    27	type MCPServerConfig struct {
    28	        // Version of the server
    29	        Version string
    30	
    31	        // GitHub Host to target for API requests (e.g. github.com or github.enterprise.com)
    32	        Host string
    33	
    34	        // GitHub Token to authenticate with the GitHub API
    35	        Token string
    36	
    37	        // EnabledToolsets is a list of toolsets to enable
    38	        // See: https://github.com/github/github-mcp-server?tab=readme-ov-file#tool-configuration
    39	        EnabledToolsets []string
    40	
    41	        // Whether to enable dynamic toolsets
    42	        // See: https://github.com/github/github-mcp-server?tab=readme-ov-file#dynamic-tool-discovery
    43	        DynamicToolsets bool
    44	
    45	        // ReadOnly indicates if we should only offer read-only tools
    46	        ReadOnly bool
    47	
    48	        // Translator provides translated text for the server tooling
    49	        Translator translations.TranslationHelperFunc
    50	}

    52	const stdioServerLogPrefix = "stdioserver"
    53	
    54	func NewMCPServer(cfg MCPServerConfig) (*server.MCPServer, error) {
    55	        apiHost, err := parseAPIHost(cfg.Host)
    56	        if err != nil {
    57	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse API host: %w", err)
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        // Construct our REST client
    61	        restClient := gogithub.NewClient(nil).WithAuthToken(cfg.Token)
    62	        restClient.UserAgent = fmt.Sprintf("github-mcp-server/%s", cfg.Version)
    63	        restClient.BaseURL = apiHost.baseRESTURL
    64	        restClient.UploadURL = apiHost.uploadURL
    65	
    66	        // Construct our GraphQL client
    67	        // We're using NewEnterpriseClient here unconditionally as opposed to NewClient because we already
    68	        // did the necessary API host parsing so that github.com will return the correct URL anyway.
    69	        gqlHTTPClient := &http.Client{
    70	                Transport: &bearerAuthTransport{
    71	                        transport: http.DefaultTransport,
    72	                        token:     cfg.Token,
    73	                },
    74	        } // We're going to wrap the Transport later in beforeInit
    75	        gqlClient := githubv4.NewEnterpriseClient(apiHost.graphqlURL.String(), gqlHTTPClient)
    76	
    77	        // When a client send an initialize request, update the user agent to include the client info.
    78	        beforeInit := func(_ context.Context, _ any, message *mcp.InitializeRequest) {
    79	                userAgent := fmt.Sprintf(
    80	                        "github-mcp-server/%s (%s/%s)",
    81	                        cfg.Version,
    82	                        message.Params.ClientInfo.Name,
    83	                        message.Params.ClientInfo.Version,
    84	                )
    85	
    86	                restClient.UserAgent = userAgent
    87	
    88	                gqlHTTPClient.Transport = &userAgentTransport{
    89	                        transport: gqlHTTPClient.Transport,
    90	                        agent:     userAgent,
    91	                }
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        hooks := &server.Hooks{
    95	                OnBeforeInitialize: []server.OnBeforeInitializeFunc{beforeInit},
    96	                OnBeforeAny: []server.BeforeAnyHookFunc{
    97	                        func(ctx context.Context, _ any, _ mcp.MCPMethod, _ any) {
    98	                                // Ensure the context is cleared of any previous errors
    99	                                // as context isn't propagated through middleware
   100	                                errors.ContextWithGitHubErrors(ctx)
   101	                        },
   102	                },
   103	        }
   104	
   105	        ghServer := github.NewServer(cfg.Version, server.WithHooks(hooks))
   106	
   107	        enabledToolsets := cfg.EnabledToolsets
   108	        if cfg.DynamicToolsets {
   109	                // filter "all" from the enabled toolsets
   110	                enabledToolsets = make([]string, 0, len(cfg.EnabledToolsets))
   111	                for _, toolset := range cfg.EnabledToolsets {
   112	                        if toolset != "all" {
   113	                                enabledToolsets = append(enabledToolsets, toolset)
   114	                        }
   115	                }
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        getClient := func(_ context.Context) (*gogithub.Client, error) {
   119	                return restClient, nil // closing over client
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        getGQLClient := func(_ context.Context) (*githubv4.Client, error) {
   123	                return gqlClient, nil // closing over client
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        getRawClient := func(ctx context.Context) (*raw.Client, error) {
   127	                client, err := getClient(ctx)
   128	                if err != nil {
   129	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
   130	                }
   131	                return raw.NewClient(client, apiHost.rawURL), nil // closing over client
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        // Create default toolsets
   135	        tsg := github.DefaultToolsetGroup(cfg.ReadOnly, getClient, getGQLClient, getRawClient, cfg.Translator)
   136	        err = tsg.EnableToolsets(enabledToolsets)
   137	
   138	        if err != nil {
   139	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to enable toolsets: %w", err)
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        // Register all mcp functionality with the server
   143	        tsg.RegisterAll(ghServer)
   144	
   145	        if cfg.DynamicToolsets {
   146	                dynamic := github.InitDynamicToolset(ghServer, tsg, cfg.Translator)
   147	                dynamic.RegisterTools(ghServer)
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        return ghServer, nil
   151	}

   153	type StdioServerConfig struct {
   154	        // Version of the server
   155	        Version string
   156	
   157	        // GitHub Host to target for API requests (e.g. github.com or github.enterprise.com)
   158	        Host string
   159	
   160	        // GitHub Token to authenticate with the GitHub API
   161	        Token string
   162	
   163	        // EnabledToolsets is a list of toolsets to enable
   164	        // See: https://github.com/github/github-mcp-server?tab=readme-ov-file#tool-configuration
   165	        EnabledToolsets []string
   166	
   167	        // Whether to enable dynamic toolsets
   168	        // See: https://github.com/github/github-mcp-server?tab=readme-ov-file#dynamic-tool-discovery
   169	        DynamicToolsets bool
   170	
   171	        // ReadOnly indicates if we should only register read-only tools
   172	        ReadOnly bool
   173	
   174	        // ExportTranslations indicates if we should export translations
   175	        // See: https://github.com/github/github-mcp-server?tab=readme-ov-file#i18n--overriding-descriptions
   176	        ExportTranslations bool
   177	
   178	        // EnableCommandLogging indicates if we should log commands
   179	        EnableCommandLogging bool
   180	
   181	        // Path to the log file if not stderr
   182	        LogFilePath string
   183	}
   184	
   185	// RunStdioServer is not concurrent safe.
   186	func RunStdioServer(cfg StdioServerConfig) error {
   187	        // Create app context
   188	        ctx, stop := signal.NotifyContext(context.Background(), os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)
   189	        defer stop()
   190	
   191	        t, dumpTranslations := translations.TranslationHelper()
   192	
   193	        ghServer, err := NewMCPServer(MCPServerConfig{
   194	                Version:         cfg.Version,
   195	                Host:            cfg.Host,
   196	                Token:           cfg.Token,
   197	                EnabledToolsets: cfg.EnabledToolsets,
   198	                DynamicToolsets: cfg.DynamicToolsets,
   199	                ReadOnly:        cfg.ReadOnly,
   200	                Translator:      t,
   201	        })
   202	        if err != nil {
   203	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to create MCP server: %w", err)
   204	        }
   205	
   206	        stdioServer := server.NewStdioServer(ghServer)
   207	
   208	        var slogHandler slog.Handler
   209	        var logOutput io.Writer
   210	        if cfg.LogFilePath != "" {
   211	                file, err := os.OpenFile(cfg.LogFilePath, os.O_CREATE|os.O_WRONLY|os.O_APPEND, 0600)
   212	                if err != nil {
   213	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to open log file: %w", err)
   214	                }
   215	                logOutput = file
   216	                slogHandler = slog.NewTextHandler(logOutput, &slog.HandlerOptions{Level: slog.LevelDebug})
   217	        } else {
   218	                logOutput = os.Stderr
   219	                slogHandler = slog.NewTextHandler(logOutput, &slog.HandlerOptions{Level: slog.LevelInfo})
   220	        }
   221	        logger := slog.New(slogHandler)
   222	        logger.Info("starting server", "version", cfg.Version, "host", cfg.Host, "dynamicToolsets", cfg.DynamicToolsets, "readOnly", cfg.ReadOnly)
   223	        stdLogger := log.New(logOutput, stdioServerLogPrefix, 0)
   224	        stdioServer.SetErrorLogger(stdLogger)
   225	
   226	        if cfg.ExportTranslations {
   227	                // Once server is initialized, all translations are loaded
   228	                dumpTranslations()
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        // Start listening for messages
   232	        errC := make(chan error, 1)
   233	        go func() {
   234	                in, out := io.Reader(os.Stdin), io.Writer(os.Stdout)
   235	
   236	                if cfg.EnableCommandLogging {
   237	                        loggedIO := mcplog.NewIOLogger(in, out, logger)
   238	                        in, out = loggedIO, loggedIO
   239	                }
   240	                // enable GitHub errors in the context
   241	                ctx := errors.ContextWithGitHubErrors(ctx)
   242	                errC <- stdioServer.Listen(ctx, in, out)
   243	        }()
   244	
   245	        // Output github-mcp-server string
   246	        _, _ = fmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, "GitHub MCP Server running on stdio\n")
   247	
   248	        // Wait for shutdown signal
   249	        select {
   250	        case <-ctx.Done():
   251	                logger.Info("shutting down server", "signal", "context done")
   252	        case err := <-errC:
   253	                if err != nil {
   254	                        logger.Error("error running server", "error", err)
   255	                        return fmt.Errorf("error running server: %w", err)
   256	                }
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        return nil
   260	}
   261	
   262	type apiHost struct {
   263	        baseRESTURL *url.URL
   264	        graphqlURL  *url.URL
   265	        uploadURL   *url.URL
   266	        rawURL      *url.URL
   267	}
   268	
   269	func newDotcomHost() (apiHost, error) {
   270	        baseRestURL, err := url.Parse("https://api.github.com/")
   271	        if err != nil {
   272	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse dotcom REST URL: %w", err)
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        gqlURL, err := url.Parse("https://api.github.com/graphql")
   276	        if err != nil {
   277	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse dotcom GraphQL URL: %w", err)
   278	        }
   279	
   280	        uploadURL, err := url.Parse("https://uploads.github.com")
   281	        if err != nil {
   282	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse dotcom Upload URL: %w", err)
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        rawURL, err := url.Parse("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/")
   286	        if err != nil {
   287	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse dotcom Raw URL: %w", err)
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        return apiHost{
   291	                baseRESTURL: baseRestURL,
   292	                graphqlURL:  gqlURL,
   293	                uploadURL:   uploadURL,
   294	                rawURL:      rawURL,
   295	        }, nil
   296	}
   297	
   298	func newGHECHost(hostname string) (apiHost, error) {
   299	        u, err := url.Parse(hostname)
   300	        if err != nil {
   301	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHEC URL: %w", err)
   302	        }
   303	
   304	        // Unsecured GHEC would be an error
   305	        if u.Scheme == "http" {
   306	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("GHEC URL must be HTTPS")
   307	        }
   308	
   309	        restURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("https://api.%s/", u.Hostname()))
   310	        if err != nil {
   311	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHEC REST URL: %w", err)
   312	        }
   313	
   314	        gqlURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("https://api.%s/graphql", u.Hostname()))
   315	        if err != nil {
   316	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHEC GraphQL URL: %w", err)
   317	        }
   318	
   319	        uploadURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("https://uploads.%s", u.Hostname()))
   320	        if err != nil {
   321	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHEC Upload URL: %w", err)
   322	        }
   323	
   324	        rawURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("https://raw.%s/", u.Hostname()))
   325	        if err != nil {
   326	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHEC Raw URL: %w", err)
   327	        }
   328	
   329	        return apiHost{
   330	                baseRESTURL: restURL,
   331	                graphqlURL:  gqlURL,
   332	                uploadURL:   uploadURL,
   333	                rawURL:      rawURL,
   334	        }, nil
   335	}
   336	
   337	func newGHESHost(hostname string) (apiHost, error) {
   338	        u, err := url.Parse(hostname)
   339	        if err != nil {
   340	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHES URL: %w", err)
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        restURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("%s://%s/api/v3/", u.Scheme, u.Hostname()))
   344	        if err != nil {
   345	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHES REST URL: %w", err)
   346	        }
   347	
   348	        gqlURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("%s://%s/api/graphql", u.Scheme, u.Hostname()))
   349	        if err != nil {
   350	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHES GraphQL URL: %w", err)
   351	        }
   352	
   353	        uploadURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("%s://%s/api/uploads/", u.Scheme, u.Hostname()))
   354	        if err != nil {
   355	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHES Upload URL: %w", err)
   356	        }
   357	        rawURL, err := url.Parse(fmt.Sprintf("%s://%s/raw/", u.Scheme, u.Hostname()))
   358	        if err != nil {
   359	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse GHES Raw URL: %w", err)
   360	        }
   361	
   362	        return apiHost{
   363	                baseRESTURL: restURL,
   364	                graphqlURL:  gqlURL,
   365	                uploadURL:   uploadURL,
   366	                rawURL:      rawURL,
   367	        }, nil
   368	}
   369	
   370	// Note that this does not handle ports yet, so development environments are out.
   371	func parseAPIHost(s string) (apiHost, error) {
   372	        if s == "" {
   373	                return newDotcomHost()
   374	        }
   375	
   376	        u, err := url.Parse(s)
   377	        if err != nil {
   378	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("could not parse host as URL: %s", s)
   379	        }
   380	
   381	        if u.Scheme == "" {
   382	                return apiHost{}, fmt.Errorf("host must have a scheme (http or https): %s", s)
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        if strings.HasSuffix(u.Hostname(), "github.com") {
   386	                return newDotcomHost()
   387	        }
   388	
   389	        if strings.HasSuffix(u.Hostname(), "ghe.com") {
   390	                return newGHECHost(s)
   391	        }
   392	
   393	        return newGHESHost(s)
   394	}
   395	
   396	type userAgentTransport struct {
   397	        transport http.RoundTripper
   398	        agent     string
   399	}
   400	
   401	func (t *userAgentTransport) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {
   402	        req = req.Clone(req.Context())
   403	        req.Header.Set("User-Agent", t.agent)
   404	        return t.transport.RoundTrip(req)
   405	}
   406	
   407	type bearerAuthTransport struct {
   408	        transport http.RoundTripper
   409	        token     string
   410	}
   411	
   412	func (t *bearerAuthTransport) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {
   413	        req = req.Clone(req.Context())
   414	        req.Header.Set("Authorization", "Bearer "+t.token)
   415	        return t.transport.RoundTrip(req)
   416	}

   107	func getIssueQueryType(hasLabels bool, hasSince bool) any {
   108	        switch {
   109	        case hasLabels && hasSince:
   110	                return &ListIssuesQueryTypeWithLabelsWithSince{}
   111	        case hasLabels:
   112	                return &ListIssuesQueryTypeWithLabels{}
   113	        case hasSince:
   114	                return &ListIssuesQueryWithSince{}
   115	        default:
   116	                return &ListIssuesQuery{}
   117	        }
   118	}
   119	
   120	func fragmentToIssue(fragment IssueFragment) *github.Issue {
   121	        // Convert GraphQL labels to GitHub API labels format
   122	        var foundLabels []*github.Label
   123	        for _, labelNode := range fragment.Labels.Nodes {
   124	                foundLabels = append(foundLabels, &github.Label{
   125	                        Name:        github.Ptr(string(labelNode.Name)),
   126	                        NodeID:      github.Ptr(string(labelNode.ID)),
   127	                        Description: github.Ptr(string(labelNode.Description)),
   128	                })
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        return &github.Issue{
   132	                Number:    github.Ptr(int(fragment.Number)),
   133	                Title:     github.Ptr(string(fragment.Title)),
   134	                CreatedAt: &github.Timestamp{Time: fragment.CreatedAt.Time},
   135	                UpdatedAt: &github.Timestamp{Time: fragment.UpdatedAt.Time},
   136	                User: &github.User{
   137	                        Login: github.Ptr(string(fragment.Author.Login)),
   138	                },
   139	                State:    github.Ptr(string(fragment.State)),
   140	                ID:       github.Ptr(fragment.DatabaseID),
   141	                Body:     github.Ptr(string(fragment.Body)),
   142	                Labels:   foundLabels,
   143	                Comments: github.Ptr(int(fragment.Comments.TotalCount)),
   144	        }
   145	}

   147	// GetIssue creates a tool to get details of a specific issue in a GitHub repository.

   330	// AddSubIssue creates a tool to add a sub-issue to a parent issue.
   331	func AddSubIssue(getClient GetClientFn, t translations.TranslationHelperFunc) (tool mcp.Tool, handler server.ToolHandlerFunc) {
   332	        return mcp.NewTool("add_sub_issue",
   333	                        mcp.WithDescription(t("TOOL_ADD_SUB_ISSUE_DESCRIPTION", "Add a sub-issue to a parent issue in a GitHub repository.")),
   334	                        mcp.WithToolAnnotation(mcp.ToolAnnotation{
   335	                                Title:        t("TOOL_ADD_SUB_ISSUE_USER_TITLE", "Add sub-issue"),
   336	                                ReadOnlyHint: ToBoolPtr(false),
   337	                        }),
   338	                        mcp.WithString("owner",
   339	                                mcp.Required(),
   340	                                mcp.Description("Repository owner"),
   341	                        ),
   342	                        mcp.WithString("repo",
   343	                                mcp.Required(),
   344	                                mcp.Description("Repository name"),
   345	                        ),
   346	                        mcp.WithNumber("issue_number",
   347	                                mcp.Required(),
   348	                                mcp.Description("The number of the parent issue"),
   349	                        ),
   350	                        mcp.WithNumber("sub_issue_id",
   351	                                mcp.Required(),
   352	                                mcp.Description("The ID of the sub-issue to add. ID is not the same as issue number"),
   353	                        ),
   354	                        mcp.WithBoolean("replace_parent",
   355	                                mcp.Description("When true, replaces the sub-issue's current parent issue"),
   356	                        ),
   357	                ),
   358	                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
   359	                        owner, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "owner")
   360	                        if err != nil {
   361	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   362	                        }
   363	                        repo, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "repo")
   364	                        if err != nil {
   365	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   366	                        }
   367	                        issueNumber, err := RequiredInt(request, "issue_number")
   368	                        if err != nil {
   369	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   370	                        }
   371	                        subIssueID, err := RequiredInt(request, "sub_issue_id")
   372	                        if err != nil {
   373	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   374	                        }
   375	                        replaceParent, err := OptionalParam[bool](request, "replace_parent")
   376	                        if err != nil {
   377	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   378	                        }
   379	
   380	                        client, err := getClient(ctx)
   381	                        if err != nil {
   382	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
   383	                        }
   384	
   385	                        subIssueRequest := github.SubIssueRequest{
   386	                                SubIssueID:    int64(subIssueID),
   387	                                ReplaceParent: ToBoolPtr(replaceParent),
   388	                        }
   389	
   390	                        subIssue, resp, err := client.SubIssue.Add(ctx, owner, repo, int64(issueNumber), subIssueRequest)
   391	                        if err != nil {
   392	                                return ghErrors.NewGitHubAPIErrorResponse(ctx,
   393	                                        "failed to add sub-issue",
   394	                                        resp,
   395	                                        err,
   396	                                ), nil
   397	                        }
   398	
   399	                        defer func() { _ = resp.Body.Close() }()
   400	
   401	                        if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusCreated {
   402	                                body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
   403	                                if err != nil {
   404	                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
   405	                                }
   406	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to add sub-issue: %s", string(body))), nil
   407	                        }
   408	
   409	                        r, err := json.Marshal(subIssue)
   410	                        if err != nil {
   411	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal response: %w", err)
   412	                        }
   413	
   414	                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(r)), nil
   415	                }
   416	}

   156	                        maintainerCanModify, err := OptionalParam[bool](request, "maintainer_can_modify")
   157	                        if err != nil {
   158	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   159	                        }
   160	
   161	                        newPR := &github.NewPullRequest{
   162	                                Title: github.Ptr(title),
   163	                                Head:  github.Ptr(head),
   164	                                Base:  github.Ptr(base),
   165	                        }
   166	
   167	                        if body != "" {
   168	                                newPR.Body = github.Ptr(body)
   169	                        }
   170	
   171	                        newPR.Draft = github.Ptr(draft)
   172	                        newPR.MaintainerCanModify = github.Ptr(maintainerCanModify)
   173	
   174	                        client, err := getClient(ctx)
   175	                        if err != nil {
   176	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
   177	                        }
   178	                        pr, resp, err := client.PullRequests.Create(ctx, owner, repo, newPR)
   179	                        if err != nil {
   180	                                return ghErrors.NewGitHubAPIErrorResponse(ctx,
   181	                                        "failed to create pull request",
   182	                                        resp,
   183	                                        err,
   184	                                ), nil
   185	                        }
   186	                        defer func() { _ = resp.Body.Close() }()
   187	
   188	                        if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusCreated {
   189	                                body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
   190	                                if err != nil {
   191	                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
   192	                                }
   193	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to create pull request: %s", string(body))), nil
   194	                        }
   195	
   196	                        r, err := json.Marshal(pr)
   197	                        if err != nil {
   198	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal response: %w", err)
   199	                        }
   200	
   201	                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(r)), nil
   202	                }
   203	}

   205	// UpdatePullRequest creates a tool to update an existing pull request.
   206	func UpdatePullRequest(getClient GetClientFn, getGQLClient GetGQLClientFn, t translations.TranslationHelperFunc) (mcp.Tool, server.ToolHandlerFunc) {
   207	        return mcp.NewTool("update_pull_request",
   208	                        mcp.WithDescription(t("TOOL_UPDATE_PULL_REQUEST_DESCRIPTION", "Update an existing pull request in a GitHub repository.")),
   209	                        mcp.WithToolAnnotation(mcp.ToolAnnotation{
   210	                                Title:        t("TOOL_UPDATE_PULL_REQUEST_USER_TITLE", "Edit pull request"),
   211	                                ReadOnlyHint: ToBoolPtr(false),
   212	                        }),
   213	                        mcp.WithString("owner",
   214	                                mcp.Required(),
   215	                                mcp.Description("Repository owner"),
   216	                        ),
   217	                        mcp.WithString("repo",
   218	                                mcp.Required(),
   219	                                mcp.Description("Repository name"),
   220	                        ),
   221	                        mcp.WithNumber("pullNumber",
   222	                                mcp.Required(),
   223	                                mcp.Description("Pull request number to update"),
   224	                        ),
   225	                        mcp.WithString("title",
   226	                                mcp.Description("New title"),
   227	                        ),
   228	                        mcp.WithString("body",
   229	                                mcp.Description("New description"),
   230	                        ),
   231	                        mcp.WithString("state",
   232	                                mcp.Description("New state"),
   233	                                mcp.Enum("open", "closed"),
   234	                        ),
   235	                        mcp.WithBoolean("draft",
   236	                                mcp.Description("Mark pull request as draft (true) or ready for review (false)"),
   237	                        ),
   238	                        mcp.WithString("base",
   239	                                mcp.Description("New base branch name"),
   240	                        ),
   241	                        mcp.WithBoolean("maintainer_can_modify",
   242	                                mcp.Description("Allow maintainer edits"),
   243	                        ),
   244	                        mcp.WithArray("reviewers",
   245	                                mcp.Description("GitHub usernames to request reviews from"),
   246	                                mcp.Items(map[string]interface{}{
   247	                                        "type": "string",
   248	                                }),
   249	                        ),
   250	                ),
   251	                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
   252	                        owner, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "owner")
   253	                        if err != nil {
   254	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   255	                        }
   256	                        repo, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "repo")
   257	                        if err != nil {
   258	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   259	                        }
   260	                        pullNumber, err := RequiredInt(request, "pullNumber")
   261	                        if err != nil {
   262	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   263	                        }
   264	
   265	                        // Check if draft parameter is provided
   266	                        draftProvided := request.GetArguments()["draft"] != nil
   267	                        var draftValue bool
   268	                        if draftProvided {
   269	                                draftValue, err = OptionalParam[bool](request, "draft")
   270	                                if err != nil {
   271	                                        return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   272	                                }
   273	                        }
   274	
   275	                        // Build the update struct only with provided fields
   276	                        update := &github.PullRequest{}
   277	                        restUpdateNeeded := false
   278	
   279	                        if title, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[string](request, "title"); err != nil {
   280	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   281	                        } else if ok {
   282	                                update.Title = github.Ptr(title)
   283	                                restUpdateNeeded = true
   284	                        }
   285	
   286	                        if body, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[string](request, "body"); err != nil {
   287	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   288	                        } else if ok {
   289	                                update.Body = github.Ptr(body)
   290	                                restUpdateNeeded = true
   291	                        }
   292	
   293	                        if state, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[string](request, "state"); err != nil {
   294	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   295	                        } else if ok {
   296	                                update.State = github.Ptr(state)
   297	                                restUpdateNeeded = true
   298	                        }
   299	
   300	                        if base, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[string](request, "base"); err != nil {
   301	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   302	                        } else if ok {
   303	                                update.Base = &github.PullRequestBranch{Ref: github.Ptr(base)}
   304	                                restUpdateNeeded = true
   305	                        }
   306	
   307	                        if maintainerCanModify, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[bool](request, "maintainer_can_modify"); err != nil {
   308	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   309	                        } else if ok {
   310	                                update.MaintainerCanModify = github.Ptr(maintainerCanModify)
   311	                                restUpdateNeeded = true
   312	                        }
   313	
   314	                        // Handle reviewers separately
   315	                        reviewers, err := OptionalStringArrayParam(request, "reviewers")
   316	                        if err != nil {
   317	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
   318	                        }
   319	
   320	                        // If no updates, no draft change, and no reviewers, return error early
   321	                        if !restUpdateNeeded && !draftProvided && len(reviewers) == 0 {
   322	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError("No update parameters provided."), nil
   323	                        }
   324	
   325	                        // Handle REST API updates (title, body, state, base, maintainer_can_modify)
   326	                        if restUpdateNeeded {
   327	                                client, err := getClient(ctx)
   328	                                if err != nil {
   329	                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
   330	                                }
   331	
   332	                                _, resp, err := client.PullRequests.Edit(ctx, owner, repo, pullNumber, update)
   333	                                if err != nil {
   334	                                        return ghErrors.NewGitHubAPIErrorResponse(ctx,
   335	                                                "failed to update pull request",
   336	                                                resp,
   337	                                                err,
   338	                                        ), nil
   339	                                }
   340	                                defer func() { _ = resp.Body.Close() }()
   341	
   342	                                if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
   343	                                        body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
   344	                                        if err != nil {
   345	                                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
   346	                                        }
   347	                                        return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to update pull request: %s", string(body))), nil
   348	                                }
   349	                        }
   350	
   351	                        // Handle draft status changes using GraphQL
   352	                        if draftProvided {
   353	                                gqlClient, err := getGQLClient(ctx)
   354	                                if err != nil {
   355	                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub GraphQL client: %w", err)
   356	                                }
   357	
   358	                                var prQuery struct {
   359	                                        Repository struct {
   360	                                                PullRequest struct {
   361	                                                        ID      githubv4.ID
   362	                                                        IsDraft githubv4.Boolean
   363	                                                } `graphql:"pullRequest(number: $prNum)"`
   364	                                        } `graphql:"repository(owner: $owner, name: $repo)"`
   365	                                }
   366	
   367	                                err = gqlClient.Query(ctx, &prQuery, map[string]interface{}{
   368	                                        "owner": githubv4.String(owner),
   369	                                        "repo":  githubv4.String(repo),
   370	                                        "prNum": githubv4.Int(pullNumber), // #nosec G115 - pull request numbers are always small positive integers
   371	                                })
   372	                                if err != nil {
   373	                                        return ghErrors.NewGitHubGraphQLErrorResponse(ctx, "Failed to find pull request", err), nil
   374	                                }
   375	
   376	                                currentIsDraft := bool(prQuery.Repository.PullRequest.IsDraft)
   377	
   378	                                if currentIsDraft != draftValue {
   379	                                        if draftValue {
   380	                                                // Convert to draft
   381	                                                var mutation struct {
   382	                                                        ConvertPullRequestToDraft struct {
   383	                                                                PullRequest struct {
   384	                                                                        ID      githubv4.ID
   385	                                                                        IsDraft githubv4.Boolean
   386	                                                                }
   387	                                                        } `graphql:"convertPullRequestToDraft(input: $input)"`
   388	                                                }
   389	
   390	                                                err = gqlClient.Mutate(ctx, &mutation, githubv4.ConvertPullRequestToDraftInput{
   391	                                                        PullRequestID: prQuery.Repository.PullRequest.ID,
   392	                                                }, nil)
   393	                                                if err != nil {
   394	                                                        return ghErrors.NewGitHubGraphQLErrorResponse(ctx, "Failed to convert pull request to draft", err), nil
   395	                                                }
   396	                                        } else {
   397	                                                // Mark as ready for review
   398	                                                var mutation struct {
   399	                                                        MarkPullRequestReadyForReview struct {
   400	                                                                PullRequest struct {
   401	                                                                        ID      githubv4.ID
   402	                                                                        IsDraft githubv4.Boolean
   403	                                                                }
   404	                                                        } `graphql:"markPullRequestReadyForReview(input: $input)"`
   405	                                                }
   406	
   407	                                                err = gqlClient.Mutate(ctx, &mutation, githubv4.MarkPullRequestReadyForReviewInput{
   408	                                                        PullRequestID: prQuery.Repository.PullRequest.ID,
   409	                                                }, nil)
   410	                                                if err != nil {
   411	                                                        return ghErrors.NewGitHubGraphQLErrorResponse(ctx, "Failed to mark pull request ready for review", err), nil
   412	                                                }
   413	                                        }
   414	                                }
   415	                        }
   416	
   417	                        // Handle reviewer requests
   418	                        if len(reviewers) > 0 {
   419	                                client, err := getClient(ctx)
   420	                                if err != nil {
   421	                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
   422	                                }
   423	
   424	                                reviewersRequest := github.ReviewersRequest{
   425	                                        Reviewers: reviewers,
   426	                                }
   427	
   428	                                _, resp, err := client.PullRequests.RequestReviewers(ctx, owner, repo, pullNumber, reviewersRequest)
   429	                                if err != nil {
   430	                                        return ghErrors.NewGitHubAPIErrorResponse(ctx,
   431	                                                "failed to request reviewers",
   432	                                                resp,
   433	                                                err,
   434	                                        ), nil
   435	                                }
   436	                                defer func() {
   437	                                        if resp != nil && resp.Body != nil {
   438	                                                _ = resp.Body.Close()
   439	                                        }
   440	                                }()
   441	
   442	                                if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusCreated && resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
   443	                                        body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
   444	                                        if err != nil {
   445	                                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
   446	                                        }
   447	                                        return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to request reviewers: %s", string(body))), nil
   448	                                }
   449	                        }
   450	
   451	                        // Get the final state of the PR to return
   452	                        client, err := getClient(ctx)
   453	                        if err != nil {
   454	                                return nil, err
   455	                        }
   456	
   457	                        finalPR, resp, err := client.PullRequests.Get(ctx, owner, repo, pullNumber)
   458	                        if err != nil {
   459	                                return ghErrors.NewGitHubAPIErrorResponse(ctx, "Failed to get pull request", resp, err), nil
   460	                        }
   461	                        defer func() {
   462	                                if resp != nil && resp.Body != nil {
   463	                                        _ = resp.Body.Close()
   464	                                }
   465	                        }()
   466	
   467	                        r, err := json.Marshal(finalPR)
   468	                        if err != nil {
   469	                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to marshal response: %v", err)), nil
   470	                        }
   471	
   472	                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(r)), nil
   473	                }
   474	}

    65	func (p *partialMock) andThen(responseHandler http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
    66	        p.t.Helper()
    67	        return func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    68	                if p.expectedPath != "" {
    69	                        require.Equal(p.t, p.expectedPath, r.URL.Path)
    70	                }
    71

    76	                        }
    77	                }

    81	                        err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&unmarshaledRequestBody)
    82	                        require.NoError(p.t, err)
    83

    85	                }
    86

    88	        }

    91	// mockResponse is a helper function to create a mock HTTP response handler

    93	func mockResponse(t *testing.T, code int, body interface{}) http.HandlerFunc {
    94	        t.Helper()
    95	        return func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
    96	                w.WriteHeader(code)
    97	                // Some tests do not expect to return a JSON object, such as fetching a raw pull request diff,
    98	                // so allow strings to be returned directly.
    99	                s, ok := body.(string)
   100	                if ok {
   101	                        _, _ = w.Write([]byte(s))
   102	                        return
   103	                }
   104	
   105	                b, err := json.Marshal(body)
   106	                require.NoError(t, err)
   107	                _, _ = w.Write(b)
   108	        }
   109	}

   165	func TestOptionalParamOK(t *testing.T) {
   166	        tests := []struct {
   167	                name        string
   168	                args        map[string]interface{}
   169	                paramName   string
   170	                expectedVal interface{}
   171	                expectedOk  bool
   172	                expectError bool
   173	                errorMsg    string
   174	        }{
   175	                {
   176	                        name:        "present and correct type (string)",
   177	                        args:        map[string]interface{}{"myParam": "hello"},
   178	                        paramName:   "myParam",
   179	                        expectedVal: "hello",
   180	                        expectedOk:  true,
   181	                        expectError: false,
   182	                },
   183	                {
   184	                        name:        "present and correct type (bool)",
   185	                        args:        map[string]interface{}{"myParam": true},
   186	                        paramName:   "myParam",
   187	                        expectedVal: true,
   188	                        expectedOk:  true,
   189	                        expectError: false,
   190	                },
   191	                {
   192	                        name:        "present and correct type (number)",
   193	                        args:        map[string]interface{}{"myParam": float64(123)},
   194	                        paramName:   "myParam",
   195	                        expectedVal: float64(123),
   196	                        expectedOk:  true,
   197	                        expectError: false,
   198	                },
   199	                {
   200	                        name:        "present but wrong type (string expected, got bool)",
   201	                        args:        map[string]interface{}{"myParam": true},
   202	                        paramName:   "myParam",
   203	                        expectedVal: "",   // Zero value for string
   204	                        expectedOk:  true, // ok is true because param exists
   205	                        expectError: true,
   206	                        errorMsg:    "parameter myParam is not of type string, is bool",
   207	                },
   208	                {
   209	                        name:        "present but wrong type (bool expected, got string)",
   210	                        args:        map[string]interface{}{"myParam": "true"},
   211	                        paramName:   "myParam",
   212	                        expectedVal: false, // Zero value for bool
   213	                        expectedOk:  true,  // ok is true because param exists
   214	                        expectError: true,
   215	                        errorMsg:    "parameter myParam is not of type bool, is string",
   216	                },
   217	                {
   218	                        name:        "parameter not present",
   219	                        args:        map[string]interface{}{"anotherParam": "value"},
   220	                        paramName:   "myParam",
   221	                        expectedVal: "", // Zero value for string
   222	                        expectedOk:  false,
   223	                        expectError: false,
   224	                },
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        for _, tc := range tests {
   228	                t.Run(tc.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   229	                        request := createMCPRequest(tc.args)
   230	
   231	                        // Test with string type assertion
   232	                        if _, isString := tc.expectedVal.(string); isString || tc.errorMsg == "parameter myParam is not of type string, is bool" {
   233	                                val, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[string](request, tc.paramName)
   234	                                if tc.expectError {
   235	                                        require.Error(t, err)
   236	                                        assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), tc.errorMsg)
   237	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedOk, ok)   // Check ok even on error
   238	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedVal, val) // Check zero value on error
   239	                                } else {
   240	                                        require.NoError(t, err)
   241	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedOk, ok)
   242	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedVal, val)
   243	                                }
   244	                        }
   245	
   246	                        // Test with bool type assertion
   247	                        if _, isBool := tc.expectedVal.(bool); isBool || tc.errorMsg == "parameter myParam is not of type bool, is string" {
   248	                                val, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[bool](request, tc.paramName)
   249	                                if tc.expectError {
   250	                                        require.Error(t, err)
   251	                                        assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), tc.errorMsg)
   252	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedOk, ok)   // Check ok even on error
   253	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedVal, val) // Check zero value on error
   254	                                } else {
   255	                                        require.NoError(t, err)
   256	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedOk, ok)
   257	                                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expectedVal, val)
   258	                                }
   259	                        }
   260	
   261	                        // Test with float64 type assertion (for number case)
   262	                        if _, isFloat := tc.expectedVal.(float64); isFloat {
   263	                                val, ok, err := OptionalParamOK[float64](request, tc.paramName)
   264	                                if tc.expectError {
   265	                                        // This case shouldn't happen for float64 in the defined tests
   266	                                        require.Fail(t, "Unexpected error case for float64")

   195	        tsg.AddToolset(gists)
   196	
   197	        return tsg
   198	}
   199	
   200	// InitDynamicToolset creates a dynamic toolset that can be used to enable other toolsets, and so requires the server and toolset group as arguments
   201	func InitDynamicToolset(s *server.MCPServer, tsg *toolsets.ToolsetGroup, t translations.TranslationHelperFunc) *toolsets.Toolset {
   202	        // Create a new dynamic toolset
   203	        // Need to add the dynamic toolset last so it can be used to enable other toolsets
   204	        dynamicToolSelection := toolsets.NewToolset("dynamic", "Discover GitHub MCP tools that can help achieve tasks by enabling additional sets of tools, you can control the enablement of any toolset to access its tools when this toolset is enabled.").
   205	                AddReadTools(
   206	                        toolsets.NewServerTool(ListAvailableToolsets(tsg, t)),
   207	                        toolsets.NewServerTool(GetToolsetsTools(tsg, t)),
   208	                        toolsets.NewServerTool(EnableToolset(s, tsg, t)),
   209	                )
   210	
   211	        dynamicToolSelection.Enabled = true
   212	        return dynamicToolSelection
   213	}
   214	
   215	// ToBoolPtr converts a bool to a *bool pointer.
   216	func ToBoolPtr(b bool) *bool {
   217	        return &b
   218	}
   219	
   220	// ToStringPtr converts a string to a *string pointer.
   221	// Returns nil if the string is empty.
   222	func ToStringPtr(s string) *string {
   223	        if s == "" {
   224	                return nil
   225	        }
   226	        return &s
   227	}

func GetIssue(getClient GetClientFn, t translations.TranslationHelperFunc) (tool mcp.Tool, handler server.ToolHandlerFunc) {' --new_str '	res := &github.Issue{
		Number:    github.Ptr(int(fragment.Number)),
		Title:     github.Ptr(string(fragment.Title)),
		CreatedAt: &github.Timestamp{Time: fragment.CreatedAt.Time},
		UpdatedAt: &github.Timestamp{Time: fragment.UpdatedAt.Time},
		User: &github.User{
			Login: github.Ptr(string(fragment.Author.Login)),
		},
		State:    github.Ptr(string(fragment.State)),
		ID:       github.Ptr(fragment.DatabaseID),
		Body:     github.Ptr(string(fragment.Body)),
		Labels:   foundLabels,
		Comments: github.Ptr(int(fragment.Comments.TotalCount)),
	}

	if fragment.IssueType.Name != "" {
		res.IssueType = &github.IssueType{Name: github.Ptr(string(fragment.IssueType.Name))}
	}

	return res
}

+        return mcp.NewTool("get_issue",
+                        mcp.WithDescription(t("TOOL_GET_ISSUE_DESCRIPTION", "Get details of a specific issue in a GitHub repository.")),
+                        mcp.WithToolAnnotation(mcp.ToolAnnotation{
+                                Title:        t("TOOL_GET_ISSUE_USER_TITLE", "Get issue details"),
+                                ReadOnlyHint: ToBoolPtr(true),
+                        }),
+                        mcp.WithString("owner",
+                                mcp.Required(),

+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("repo",
+                                mcp.Required(),

+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithNumber("issue_number",
+                                mcp.Required(),
+                                mcp.Description("The number of the issue"),
+                        ),
+                ),
+                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
+                        owner, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "owner")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        repo, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "repo")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        issueNumber, err := RequiredInt(request, "issue_number")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        client, err := getClient(ctx)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        issue, resp, err := client.Issues.Get(ctx, owner, repo, issueNumber)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get issue: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        defer func() { _ = resp.Body.Close() }()
+
+                        if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+                                body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
+                                }
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to get issue: %s", string(body))), nil
+                        }
+
+                        r, err := json.Marshal(issue)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal issue: %w", err)
+                        }
+
+                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(r)), nil
+                }
 }

+                        mcp.WithNumber("issue_number",
+                                mcp.Required(),
+                                mcp.Description("The number of the parent issue"),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithNumber("sub_issue_id",
+                                mcp.Required(),
+                                mcp.Description("The ID of the sub-issue to add. ID is not the same as issue number"),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithBoolean("replace_parent",
+                                mcp.Description("When true, replaces the sub-issue's current parent issue"),
+                        ),
+                ),
+                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
+                        owner, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "owner")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        repo, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "repo")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        issueNumber, err := RequiredInt(request, "issue_number")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        subIssueID, err := RequiredInt(request, "sub_issue_id")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        replaceParent, err := OptionalParam[bool](request, "replace_parent")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        client, err := getClient(ctx)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
+                        }
+
+                        subIssueRequest := github.SubIssueRequest{
+                                SubIssueID:    int64(subIssueID),
+                                ReplaceParent: ToBoolPtr(replaceParent),
+                        }
+
+                        subIssue, resp, err := client.SubIssue.Add(ctx, owner, repo, int64(issueNumber), subIssueRequest)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return ghErrors.NewGitHubAPIErrorResponse(ctx,
+                                        "failed to add sub-issue",
+                                        resp,
+                                        err,
+                                ), nil
+                        }
+
+                        defer func() { _ = resp.Body.Close() }()
+
+                        if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusCreated {
+                                body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
+                                }
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to add sub-issue: %s", string(body))), nil
+                        }
+
+                        r, err := json.Marshal(subIssue)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal response: %w", err)
+                        }
+
+                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(r)), nil
+                }
 }

+                                Title:        t("TOOL_SEARCH_ISSUES_USER_TITLE", "Search issues"),
+                                ReadOnlyHint: ToBoolPtr(true),
+                        }),
+                        mcp.WithString("query",
+                                mcp.Required(),
+                                mcp.Description("Search query using GitHub issues search syntax"),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("owner",
+                                mcp.Description("Optional repository owner. If provided with repo, only issues for this repository are listed."),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("repo",
+                                mcp.Description("Optional repository name. If provided with owner, only issues for this repository are listed."),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("sort",
+                                mcp.Description("Sort field by number of matches of categories, defaults to best match"),
+                                mcp.Enum(
+                                        "comments",
+                                        "reactions",
+                                        "reactions-+1",
+                                        "reactions--1",
+                                        "reactions-smile",
+                                        "reactions-thinking_face",
+                                        "reactions-heart",
+                                        "reactions-tada",
+                                        "interactions",
+                                        "created",
+                                        "updated",
+                                ),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("order",
+                                mcp.Description("Sort order"),
+                                mcp.Enum("asc", "desc"),
+                        ),
+                        WithPagination(),
+                ),
+                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
+                        return searchHandler(ctx, getClient, request, "issue", "failed to search issues")
+                }
 }

+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithArray("assignees",
+                                mcp.Description("Usernames to assign to this issue"),
+                                mcp.Items(
+                                        map[string]any{
+                                                "type": "string",
+                                        },
+                                ),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithArray("labels",
+                                mcp.Description("Labels to apply to this issue"),
+                                mcp.Items(
+                                        map[string]any{
+                                                "type": "string",
+                                        },
+                                ),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithNumber("milestone",
+                                mcp.Description("Milestone number"),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("issue_type",
+                                mcp.Description("The type of issue (e.g. feature, bug, task)"),
+                        ),
+                ),
+                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
+                        owner, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "owner")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        repo, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "repo")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        title, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "title")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Optional parameters
+                        body, err := OptionalParam[string](request, "body")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Get assignees
+                        assignees, err := OptionalStringArrayParam(request, "assignees")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Get labels
+                        labels, err := OptionalStringArrayParam(request, "labels")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Get optional milestone
+                        milestone, err := OptionalIntParam(request, "milestone")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        // Get optional issue type
+                        issueType, err := OptionalParam[string](request, "issue_type")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+
+                        var milestoneNum *int
+                        if milestone != 0 {
+                                milestoneNum = &milestone
+                        }
+
+                        // Create the issue request
+                        issueRequest := &github.IssueRequest{
+                                Title:     github.Ptr(title),
+                                Body:      github.Ptr(body),
+                                Assignees: &assignees,
+                                Labels:    &labels,
+                                Milestone: milestoneNum,
+                                IssueType:  github.Ptr(issueType),
+                        }
+
+                        client, err := getClient(ctx)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get GitHub client: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        issue, resp, err := client.Issues.Create(ctx, owner, repo, issueRequest)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create issue: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        defer func() { _ = resp.Body.Close() }()
+
+                        if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusCreated {
+                                body, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read response body: %w", err)
+                                }
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to create issue: %s", string(body))), nil
+                        }
+
+                        r, err := json.Marshal(issue)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal response: %w", err)
+                        }
+
+                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(r)), nil
+                }
 }

+                                mcp.Description("Repository name"),

+                                mcp.Enum("OPEN", "CLOSED"),

+                        mcp.WithArray("labels",
+                                mcp.Description("Filter by labels"),

+                                mcp.Enum("CREATED_AT", "UPDATED_AT", "COMMENTS"),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("direction",
+                                mcp.Description("Order direction. If provided, the 'orderBy' also needs to be provided."),
+                                mcp.Enum("ASC", "DESC"),
+                        ),
+                        mcp.WithString("since",
+                                mcp.Description("Filter by date (ISO 8601 timestamp)"),

+                        WithCursorPagination(),
+                ),
+                func(ctx context.Context, request mcp.CallToolRequest) (*mcp.CallToolResult, error) {
+                        owner, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "owner")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+                        repo, err := RequiredParam[string](request, "repo")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Set optional parameters if provided
+                        state, err := OptionalParam[string](request, "state")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // If the state has a value, cast into an array of strings
+                        var states []githubv4.IssueState
+                        if state != "" {
+                                states = append(states, githubv4.IssueState(state))
+                        } else {
+                                states = []githubv4.IssueState{githubv4.IssueStateOpen, githubv4.IssueStateClosed}
+                        }
+
+                        // Get labels
+                        labels, err := OptionalStringArrayParam(request, "labels")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        orderBy, err := OptionalParam[string](request, "orderBy")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        direction, err := OptionalParam[string](request, "direction")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // These variables are required for the GraphQL query to be set by default
+                        // If orderBy is empty, default to CREATED_AT
+                        if orderBy == "" {
+                                orderBy = "CREATED_AT"
+                        }
+                        // If direction is empty, default to DESC
+                        if direction == "" {
+                                direction = "DESC"
+                        }
+
+                        since, err := OptionalParam[string](request, "since")
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // There are two optional parameters: since and labels.
+                        var sinceTime time.Time
+                        var hasSince bool
+                        if since != "" {
+                                sinceTime, err = parseISOTimestamp(since)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to list issues: %s", err.Error())), nil
+                                }
+                                hasSince = true
+                        }
+                        hasLabels := len(labels) > 0
+
+                        // Get pagination parameters and convert to GraphQL format
+                        pagination, err := OptionalCursorPaginationParams(request)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, err
+                        }
+
+                        // Check if someone tried to use page-based pagination instead of cursor-based
+                        if _, pageProvided := request.GetArguments()["page"]; pageProvided {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError("This tool uses cursor-based pagination. Use the 'after' parameter with the 'endCursor' value from the previous response instead of 'page'."), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Check if pagination parameters were explicitly provided
+                        _, perPageProvided := request.GetArguments()["perPage"]
+                        paginationExplicit := perPageProvided
+
+                        paginationParams, err := pagination.ToGraphQLParams()
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, err
+                        }
+
+                        // Use default of 30 if pagination was not explicitly provided
+                        if !paginationExplicit {
+                                defaultFirst := int32(DefaultGraphQLPageSize)
+                                paginationParams.First = &defaultFirst
+                        }
+
+                        client, err := getGQLClient(ctx)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(fmt.Sprintf("failed to get GitHub GQL client: %v", err)), nil
+                        }
+
+                        vars := map[string]interface{}{
+                                "owner":     githubv4.String(owner),
+                                "repo":      githubv4.String(repo),
+                                "states":    states,
+                                "orderBy":   githubv4.IssueOrderField(orderBy),
+                                "direction": githubv4.OrderDirection(direction),
+                                "first":     githubv4.Int(*paginationParams.First),
+                        }
+
+                        if paginationParams.After != nil {
+                                vars["after"] = githubv4.String(*paginationParams.After)
+                        } else {
+                                // Used within query, therefore must be set to nil and provided as $after
+                                vars["after"] = (*githubv4.String)(nil)
+                        }
+
+                        // Ensure optional parameters are set
+                        if hasLabels {
+                                // Use query with labels filtering - convert string labels to githubv4.String slice
+                                labelStrings := make([]githubv4.String, len(labels))
+                                for i, label := range labels {
+                                        labelStrings[i] = githubv4.String(label)
+                                }
+                                vars["labels"] = labelStrings
+                        }
+
+                        if hasSince {
+                                vars["since"] = githubv4.DateTime{Time: sinceTime}
+                        }
+
+                        issueQuery := getIssueQueryType(hasLabels, hasSince)
+                        if err := client.Query(ctx, issueQuery, vars); err != nil {
+                                return mcp.NewToolResultError(err.Error()), nil
+                        }
+
+                        // Extract and convert all issue nodes using the common interface
+                        var issues []*github.Issue
+                        var pageInfo struct {
+                                HasNextPage     githubv4.Boolean
+                                HasPreviousPage githubv4.Boolean
+                                StartCursor     githubv4.String
+                                EndCursor       githubv4.String
+                        }
+                        var totalCount int
+
+                        if queryResult, ok := issueQuery.(IssueQueryResult); ok {
+                                fragment := queryResult.GetIssueFragment()
+                                for _, issue := range fragment.Nodes {
+                                        issues = append(issues, fragmentToIssue(issue))
+                                }
+                                pageInfo = fragment.PageInfo
+                                totalCount = fragment.TotalCount
+                        }
+
+                        // Create response with issues
+                        response := map[string]interface{}{
+                                "issues": issues,
+                                "pageInfo": map[string]interface{}{
+                                        "hasNextPage":     pageInfo.HasNextPage,
+                                        "hasPreviousPage": pageInfo.HasPreviousPage,
+                                        "startCursor":     string(pageInfo.StartCursor),
+                                        "endCursor":       string(pageInfo.EndCursor),
+                                },
+                                "totalCount": totalCount,
+                        }
+                        out, err := json.Marshal(response)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal issues: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        return mcp.NewToolResultText(string(out)), nil
+                }
 }
